# **THE COMPLETE VML ASTRONOMICAL & ASTROLOGICAL SECTION**

## **Full EVA Transcription, VML Translation, Visual Analysis & Plain-Language Understanding**

### **Folios f58r through f73v — The Voynich Manuscript's Cosmological Infrastructure & Zodiac Month-Wheels**

---

## **HOW TO READ THIS DOCUMENT**

This section covers the manuscript's ASTRONOMICAL AND ASTROLOGICAL pages — the timing and scheduling infrastructure that governs when and how all pharmaceutical operations are executed. It includes:

* **Cosmological reference texts** (f58r, f65v) — Master specifications defining the temporal architecture.  
* **Astronomical diagrams** (f66r–f69r) — Calendar wheels, stellar references, and constellation maps.  
* **The Four Master Wheels** (f67r1, f67r2, f67v1, f67v2) — The scheduling command center: lunar calendar, planetary program, solar timing, and elemental configuration.  
* **Zodiac month-wheels** (f70r2–f73v) — Individual operational schedules for each of 12 zodiac months, encoding daily production parameters as nymph-labels (degree-addresses).

**Structural Note:** The zodiac pages (f70–f73) exist on FOLD-OUT sheets that are read as paired wheels (dark half / light half of each month). Some zodiac wheels are only partially preserved in the EVA interlinear transcription; where available, the Complete VML Astrological Section Translation supplements the base EVA data.

Each folio entry contains five sections, identical to the Herbal document:

1. **EVA TRANSCRIPTION** — Raw Voynichese line-by-line  
2. **VML TOKEN TRANSLATION** — Morpheme-level decode  
3. **OPERATIONAL TRANSLATION** — Process-flow reading  
4. **IMAGE/DIAGRAM DESCRIPTION & STRUCTURAL ANALYSIS** — What the diagram looks like and what each visual element means  
5. **PLAIN-LANGUAGE UNDERSTANDING** — Everyday explanation

**Astrological VML Quick Reference (additions to Herbal):**

* **ot-** \= temporal-drive (SCHEDULING — the most important astrological prefix)  
* **ok-** \= phase-shift (TRANSITION between states)  
* **of-** \= formative-source (VEGETATIVE/GROWTH force — tracks Venus)  
* **\-al** \= structure/matrix (BUILDING — dominant in Earth signs)  
* **\-am** \= union/vessel (JOINING — marks completion/conjunction)  
* **\-aiin** \= double-life-cycle (FULL CYCLE completion)  
* **CKH/KCH** \= valve/clamp (FLOW CONTROL — appears in every zodiac sign)

**The Five-Tier Hypertext Architecture:**

* **Tier 1 (f67r2):** Master Scheduler — WHEN (planetary governance)  
* **Tier 2 (f70–f73):** 30-step monthly sequences — WHAT sequence  
* **Tier 3 (recipe stars):** Cross-reference index — WHERE  
* **Tier 4A (herbal):** Plant diagrams — HOW (simple serial)  
* **Tier 4B (bath):** Pool-pipe-nymph diagrams — HOW (complex network)  
* **Tier 5 (pharmaceutical):** Recipe steps — HOW MUCH and IN WHAT ORDER

---

## **3\. Operational Translation (Process Flow)**

**Line 1 (P.1):** \[cphy\] → FORMATIVE/VEGETATIVE → checfhy → FIX/STABILIZE → y-dchepain → \[active/energized\] → TRANSITION-ESSENCE → ty → TRANSMUTE-FLUID → y → \[active/energized\] → FORMATIVE/VEGETATIVE → fluid → CHANNEL/SPIRIT → pdy

**Line 2 (P.2):** FIX/STABILIZE → double-life-cycle → TRANSITION-ESSENCE → ek → HEAT/ACTIVATE → dy-yteo → \[fixed/stabilized\] → TRANSMUTE-FLUID → s → complete-root → VOLATILE-ESSENCE → temporal → FIX/STABILIZE → structure/matrix → \[vessel\]

**Line 3 (P.3):** MOIST-ENERGY → structure/matrix → VOLATILE-ESSENCE → temporal → VIGOROUS-FLOW/TRANSITION → moist-active → RECEPTIVE/MOIST → \-sas → VOLATILE-ESSENCE → heat-fix → \[active/energized\]

**Line 4 (P.4):** ENERGY/TEMPORAL → oeedy → TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → source/rotation → TRANSITION-ESSENCE → dy-yteey → \[fixed/stabilized\] → TRANSITION-ESSENCE → heat-fix → \[active/energized\] → EXTRACT-ESSENCE → shd → RECEPTIVE/MOIST → fchey

**Line 5 (P.5):** FIX-TRANSITION → edy → \[essence-fixed\] → PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → eody → EXTRACT-ESSENCE → d-shckhy → VOLATILE-HEAT → moist-active → VOLATILE-HEAT → keody → PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → e → RECEPTIVE/MOIST → dy → \[fixed/stabilized\]

**Line 6 (P.6):** TRANSMUTE/CIRCULATE → MOIST-ENERGY → chey → VIGOROUS-FLOW/TRANSITION → ckhecphy-ykchedy → VOLATILE-ESSENCE → dy → \[fixed/stabilized\] → VIGOROUS-FLOW/TRANSITION → ckhdy

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Physical Structure:** Six short text lines with stem dividers. Fragmentary — possibly surviving edge of a larger folio.

**Description:** Six short paired phrases separated by stem-marks ({stem} notation in EVA). Each line contains a brief process command followed by a product/state descriptor. The format is CALL-AND-RESPONSE: operation → result, operation → result. Heavy qo- (circulate) and \-dy (fixed) morphemes.

**VML Structural Decode:** Text-only fragment with PAIRED STRUCTURE — each half-line is an operation-result couplet. This format matches alchemical recipe shorthand where each step names both the action and the expected outcome. The stem dividers literally separate CAUSE from EFFECT.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This is an astronomical reference page that helps calibrate the timing system used to schedule pharmaceutical operations. Medieval practitioners believed that the effectiveness of medicines depended on WHEN they were prepared — which planet was dominant, which zodiac sign was active, whether the moon was waxing or waning. This page provides reference data (star positions, phase markers, calibration points) that the practitioner needs to correctly TIME their work according to the celestial calendar.

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Physical Structure:** Large circular diagram with concentric rings of text and labels. 82 text segments including ring labels (L), ring text (R), star labels (S), paragraph (P), and individual text markers.

**Description:** Large circular astronomical diagram with multiple concentric text rings. Approximately 30+ labels (L-series) positioned around and within the rings. The outermost ring contains continuous text. Inner rings contain shorter label sequences. Central area contains additional labels or symbols. This is one of the most densely labeled pages in the manuscript — a SCHEDULING WHEEL or CALENDAR DEVICE with multiple data tracks.

**VML Structural Decode:** MULTI-RING CALENDAR WHEEL — each concentric ring represents a different time scale or data track. Outer ring \= macro-cycle (yearly/seasonal), inner rings \= progressively finer divisions. Labels at intersections \= ADDRESSES where specific operations are triggered. The multiple label-series (L1-L30+) provide the LOOKUP TABLE for the scheduling system — analogous to column headers in a spreadsheet.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This is an astronomical reference page that helps calibrate the timing system used to schedule pharmaceutical operations. Medieval practitioners believed that the effectiveness of medicines depended on WHEN they were prepared — which planet was dominant, which zodiac sign was active, whether the moon was waxing or waning. This page provides reference data (star positions, phase markers, calibration points) that the practitioner needs to correctly TIME their work according to the celestial calendar. The text contains 13 completion markers, confirming this is a structured multi-step system with clear checkpoints.

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Physical Structure:** Circular diagram continuation with text rings and labels. 13 text segments.

**Description:** Continuation of the circular astronomical diagram from f66r (facing page). Additional text rings and labels complete the scheduling wheel. Shorter text than f66r suggests this is the "back" or "answer" side of the paired diagram — where f66r defines the schedule, f66v may encode the EXECUTION RULES.

**VML Structural Decode:** PAIRED COMPLEMENT to f66r — together they form a complete two-page scheduling spread. The reduced text density suggests this page provides DERIVED VALUES or SECONDARY CALCULATIONS based on the primary schedule in f66r.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This is an astronomical reference page that helps calibrate the timing system used to schedule pharmaceutical operations. Medieval practitioners believed that the effectiveness of medicines depended on WHEN they were prepared — which planet was dominant, which zodiac sign was active, whether the moon was waxing or waning. This page provides reference data (star positions, phase markers, calibration points) that the practitioner needs to correctly TIME their work according to the celestial calendar. The text contains 4 completion markers, confirming this is a structured multi-step system with clear checkpoints.

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Physical Structure:** Circular diagram with moon-face center, 12 month sectors. Three concentric text rings (R1-R3). Internal labels and paragraph text.

**Description:** Central moon-face surrounded by 12 radial sectors representing months or lunar divisions. Three concentric rings of Voynichese text wrap around the diagram. The moon face has identifiable features (eyes, nose, mouth drawn). Sectors are separated by radial lines. Each sector contains or aligns with text from the ring system. A paragraph of text appears below or beside the diagram.

**VML Structural Decode:** LUNAR MONTH-WHEEL — the central moon face identifies this as the LUNAR scheduling system. 12 sectors \= 12 months or 12 lunar cycles. R1 (outer) \= MACRO-ENVIRONMENT rules (what conditions prevail). R2 (middle) \= PROCESS CORRIDOR (what operations run). R3 (inner) \= KERNEL TIMING (irreducible timing atom). The paragraph (P) provides the INITIALIZATION SEQUENCE — instructions for how to read and use the wheel. This is Tier 1 of the Five-Tier Hypertext: the MASTER SCHEDULER that answers WHEN.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page is the MASTER CALENDAR — the central scheduling diagram that governs the entire year's worth of pharmaceutical operations. The circular diagram divides the year into 12 phases (months), and assigns a governing planet to each phase. The practitioner would consult this page FIRST to determine what kind of operations are appropriate for the current time period. It functions exactly like a modern production scheduler — telling a factory manager which product lines to run based on the calendar. The text contains 6 completion markers, confirming this is a structured multi-step system with clear checkpoints.

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Physical Structure:** Circular diagram with 12 wedge sectors, moon faces, RED Voynichese text (unique in entire manuscript). Label systems: L (7 planet labels), X (12 under moons), Y (12 red sector headings), Z (8 central star labels). Paragraph below.

**Description:** The ONLY folio in the entire Voynich Manuscript with Voynichese text written in RED INK — all other text is brown/dark. Circular diagram divided into 12 wedge sectors with alternating light/dark moon-like faces. Ruling lines visible (very rare in the MS). The red ink labels form a hierarchy: 12 outer sector headings (Y-series, in red), 12 labels under moon faces (X-series, in black), 7 planetary labels (L-series), and 8 labels around a central star (Z-series). A paragraph in standard brown ink appears below the diagram.

**VML Structural Decode:** RED-INK HIERARCHICAL PROGRAM — the unique use of red ink creates a THREE-LEVEL ENCODING HIERARCHY: RED Y-labels \= MACRO phase titles (the "chapter headings" of the year), BLACK X-labels \= micro-clauses (specific operational addresses within each phase), L-labels \= the 7 classical planets (timing governors). Z-labels at center \= the 8-point ANCHOR SYSTEM (cardinal/ordinal reference points). The 7/12/12/8 count structure is stable across all facsimiles. This page IS the planetary control program — it assigns which planet governs which phase of the annual cycle.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page is the MASTER CALENDAR — the central scheduling diagram that governs the entire year's worth of pharmaceutical operations. It is the ONLY page in the entire manuscript with text written in RED INK, making it the most hierarchically important page in the document. The circular diagram divides the year into 12 phases (months), and assigns a governing planet to each phase. The practitioner would consult this page FIRST to determine what kind of operations are appropriate for the current time period. It functions exactly like a modern production scheduler — telling a factory manager which product lines to run based on the calendar. The text contains 12 completion markers, confirming this is a structured multi-step system with clear checkpoints.

---

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Physical Structure:** Central orb with cross dividing circle into 4 quadrants (N-S-E-W). Two face-circles (NE, SE). Four arms extending to face-clusters. Concentric text rings (R1-R3). Circular titles (C1-C4). Diagram labels.

**Description:** A CROSS-QUARTERED WHEEL with a central orb encircled by a green band. A drawn cross divides the circle into four quadrants aligned to cardinal directions (N-S-E-W). At NE and SE positions are small circles containing drawn faces (face-nodi), each with short labels. The four cross-arms extend to external pipe/channel terminations bearing clusters of small faces or disks — commonly 4, 4, 4, and 3 faces, implying quarter-phase distinctions. Dot-chains connect features back to controlling luminaries (sun vs. moon). Three concentric text rings surround the diagram. Four circular title labels sit at cardinal positions.

**VML Structural Decode:** FOUR-ELEMENT / FOUR-DIRECTION MAPPING — the cross-quartered structure maps the four classical elements (Earth/Water/Air/Fire) to spatial directions and temporal phases. The two face-nodi \= SUN and MOON as governing luminaries. The four arm-clusters \= the four TIDES or FORCES that drive material circulation. This is the ENVIRONMENT CONFIGURATION page — it sets the elemental context within which all zodiac operations execute. Medieval parallels include four-wind diagrams and four-humor schematics. Text rings provide the OPERATING PARAMETERS for each quadrant.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page shows a FOUR-DIRECTIONS MAP — a diagram that organizes the four classical elements (Earth, Water, Air, Fire) according to compass directions. For a medieval practitioner, this wasn't just geography — it defined which ELEMENTAL FORCES were active depending on orientation, season, and time of day. It sets the environmental CONTEXT within which all laboratory operations take place. Think of it as a CONFIGURATION SETTINGS page — before you run any procedure, you consult this to know what baseline conditions are in effect.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This is an astronomical reference page that helps calibrate the timing system used to schedule pharmaceutical operations. # **FOLIO F68V2 — VERSO (sub-page 2\)**

**Section:** PLANETARY ORBIT LABELS **Function:** PLANETARY PARAMETER TABLE — converts orbital positions into operational timing parameters.

## **1\. EVA Transcription**

**C.1** \[Circular Title\]: `shsdy.dalchos.okos.cheky.otees.otas.oteydy.okechoy.` **C.2** \[Circular Title\]: `yteody.cheady.cheectheey.otychdy.oteey.` **C.3** \[Circular Title\]: `cpheeody.oteil.chkey.daiin.chey.daiir.oteeys.sar.ockheey.` **C.4** \[Circular Title\]: `diiirrchy.okchil.qokeechy.dal.chy.chokeey.sary.okeadaiin.ykeeody.` **P.1** \[Paragraph\]: `teeody.shcthey.psheody.shocthy.ykeody.shdy.shot.ytchy-` **P.2** \[Paragraph\]: `dchaiin.shey.dcheedy.qokeey.shckhy.dal.dy.shecthey.daldy-` **P.3** \[Paragraph\]: `qoeeey.shekeey.shkeey.s.alchey.cthy.shteody.qoteeody.dam-` **P.4** \[Paragraph\]: `okeey.sheoy.keol.ych*ty.okeody.shey.qokey.chol.chekody-` **P.5** \[Paragraph\]: `scheos.shekey.okey.chody.okeos.cheo.salar.allchdm=` **R.1** \[Ring Text\]: `otey.daliir={12:30}` **R.10** \[Ring Text\]: `ychedal.daiin={9:30}` **R.11** \[Ring Text\]: `ilkeeepol-{star}yypchy={10:30}` **R.12** \[Ring Text\]: `choteey.dariiir={11:30}` **R.2** \[Ring Text\]: `otosey-{star}sary={1:30}` **R.3** \[Ring Text\]: `yshesas.ar.shy={2:30}` **R.4** \[Ring Text\]: `siiircthr.chety={3:30}` **R.5** \[Ring Text\]: `oteoys-{star}oraraly={4:30}` **R.6** \[Ring Text\]: `yteody.chetey={5:30}` **R.7** \[Ring Text\]: `otchos.alamchy={6:30}` **R.8** \[Ring Text\]: `otchdy-{star}chetal={7:30}` **R.9** \[Ring Text\]: `adairchdy.aiin={8:30}`

## **2\. VML Token Translation**

**C.1:** shsdy \= VIGOROUS-FLOW/TRANSITION → sdy; dalchos \= FIX/STABILIZE → structure/matrix; okos \= PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → os; cheky \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → moist-active; otees \= TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → essence-energy; otas \= TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → as; oteydy \= TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → essence-active → \[fixed/stabilized\]; okechoy \= PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → echoy

**C.2:** yteody \= MOIST-ENERGY → eody; cheady \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → ady; cheectheey \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → ectheey; otychdy \= TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → ychdy → \[active/energized\]; oteey \= TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → essence-active

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Physical Structure:** Diagram with 21 text segments — likely concentric orbital rings with labels.

**Description:** Complex diagram with 21 text labels arranged around orbital ring structures. Labels include planetary names and orbital parameter specifications. The high label count suggests detailed orbital characterization — positions, velocities, or influence strengths for each planetary body across different positions.

**VML Structural Decode:** PLANETARY ORBIT PARAMETER TABLE — each label specifies a planetary position or influence-state. The 21 labels may represent the 7 planets × 3 states (e.g., ascending/stationed/descending, or domicile/exaltation/fall). VML decode shows alternations of d- (fix), s- (salt/flowing), and o- (heat) corresponding to orbital dynamics. This page converts planetary geometry into operational parameters — identical alchemical grammar applied at cosmic scale.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This is an astronomical reference page that helps calibrate the timing system used to schedule pharmaceutical operations. Medieval practitioners believed that the effectiveness of medicines depended on WHEN they were prepared — which planet was dominant, which zodiac sign was active, whether the moon was waxing or waning. This page provides reference data (star positions, phase markers, calibration points) that the practitioner needs to correctly TIME their work according to the celestial calendar.

The text establishes default parameters, safety limits, and operational rules that apply universally across all 12 zodiac months. Labels include both paragraph text and ring text from the associated Pisces diagram.

**VML Structural Decode:** ZODIAC BOOT CODE — the paragraph sets universal parameters (default temperatures, pressures, durations) that all month-wheels inherit. Ring text encodes the OUTER LAW — the environmental constraints within which all operations must occur. This is the equivalent of a CONFIG FILE that runs before any monthly subroutine.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page is a ZODIAC MONTH-WHEEL — a circular calendar diagram that tells a medieval alchemist or pharmacist exactly what to do on each day of a specific month. The sign is Pisces (DARK half) — February/March opening Each naked figure (nymph) in the diagram represents ONE DAY of the month. The label next to each nymph is a coded instruction set — it tells the practitioner what operation to perform (heating, extracting, mixing), on what material, and to what target state (stable, fluid, active). The concentric text rings around the wheel encode environmental rules (what temperature, what humidity, what celestial conditions are in effect) that modify every daily operation. Think of it as a DAILY PLANNER for a pharmaceutical laboratory, where every day's task is precisely scheduled according to astrological timing. The text contains 4 completion markers, confirming this is a structured multi-step system with clear checkpoints.

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Physical Structure:** Zodiac wheel with fish emblem at center. Two concentric nymph bands: S1 outer (10-15 nymphs), S2 inner (5-10 nymphs). Three text rings (R1-R3). Nymph labels. Male figure present.

**Description:** Circular zodiac wheel with FISH emblem at center (identifying Pisces). Naked female figures (nymphs) arranged in two concentric bands — outer band has \~15 figures, inner band has \~10 figures. Each nymph holds a star or stands near a star symbol. One figure is distinctly MALE with beard (the "operator" or "valve controller"). Three concentric text rings wrap around the wheel. Nymph labels provide degree-addresses (each nymph \= one degree-day of the month). Stars are mixed 6-pointed and 7-pointed. Some nymphs reach toward barrels or containers.

**VML Structural Decode:** PISCES MONTH-WHEEL — each nymph is a DEGREE-ADDRESS encoding one day's operational parameters. The OUTER BAND nymphs \= the main operational schedule (what to do each day). The INNER BAND nymphs \= sub-phase refinements (micro-timing within each day). The MALE FIGURE \= the VALVE OPERATOR — the process control point where flow must be manually regulated (always positioned at the CKH/valve morpheme). Stars \= quality/intensity markers. Barrels \= containment vessels. Rings encode: R1 \= macro environment, R2 \= process corridor, R3 \= kernel timing. PISCES as Water sign drives DISSOLUTION and PHASE TRANSITIONS — ot- (temporal) is the dominant prefix (14 occurrences). Jupiter rules: y- (receptive) and f- (formative) atoms present.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page is a ZODIAC MONTH-WHEEL — a circular calendar diagram that tells a medieval alchemist or pharmacist exactly what to do on each day of a specific month. The sign is Pisces — Water/Mutable/Jupiter. Final sign. TIMING is fundamental (ot- dominant). Completes cycle by FIXING what was ACTIVATED throughout year. Each naked figure (nymph) in the diagram represents ONE DAY of the month. The label next to each nymph is a coded instruction set — it tells the practitioner what operation to perform (heating, extracting, mixing), on what material, and to what target state (stable, fluid, active). The concentric text rings around the wheel encode environmental rules (what temperature, what humidity, what celestial conditions are in effect) that modify every daily operation. Think of it as a DAILY PLANNER for a pharmaceutical laboratory, where every day's task is precisely scheduled according to astrological timing.

# **FOLIO F71V — VERSO**

**Section:** ZODIAC — TAURUS **Zodiac:** Taurus — Earth/Fixed/Venus. Neck/throat. Exaltation of Moon (3°). Stable earth, generative force. **Function:** TAURUS OPERATIONAL WHEEL — 15 degree-addresses. Peak Venus force. Maximum equipment complexity.

## **2\. VML Token Translation**

**R3.1:** kal \= BODY/CONTAIN → structure/matrix; okeey \= PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → essence-active; okeosar \= PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → eosar; otaiin \= TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → double-life-cycle; chkeeal \= CHANNEL/SPIRIT → keeal; okal \= PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → structure/matrix; cheekaiin \= VOLATILE-ESSENCE → ekaiin; okaiin \= PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → double-life-cycle; okshor \= PHASE-SHIFT/HEAT-ESSENCE → vigorous-flow-source; dar \= FIX/STABILIZE → root/projection; oteey \= TEMPORAL-DRIVE/HEAT-ENERGY → essence-active

## **4\. Diagram Description & Structural Analysis**

**Physical Structure:** Zodiac wheel with bull emblem. Two nymph bands: S1 outer (10 labels), S2 inner (5 labels). Text rings (R2-R3). Total 15 nymphs.

**Description:** Circular zodiac wheel with BULL emblem at center (identifying Taurus). 15 nymphs arranged in two bands — 10 outer, 5 inner. Nymphs show mixed states of dress and undress. Some hold objects. Text rings provide operational parameters. Contains the ONLY double-F token (ofacfom) in the entire zodiac section — maximum vegetative/growth force. Dense apparatus vocabulary (shepchol, shopcho \= distillation equipment terms).

**VML Structural Decode:** TAURUS MONTH-WHEEL — Earth/Fixed/Venus. 15 degree-addresses. Venus rules: f-atom (formative/vegetative) count is HIGHEST of any sign (3 occurrences). The bull that HOLDS GROUND — al (structure), ar (root), \-dy (fixed) dominate labels. Earth signs BUILD and FIX. Taurus has the densest APPARATUS vocabulary of any zodiac page, suggesting this month involves the most complex equipment setup. The double-F token marks MAXIMUM GROWTH FORCE — the peak of Venus's productive power. Inner nymphs in barrels \= contained/bound processes. Outer free nymphs \= active/fluid processes.

## **5\. Plain-Language Understanding**

This page is a ZODIAC MONTH-WHEEL — a circular calendar diagram that tells a medieval alchemist or pharmacist exactly what to do on each day of a specific month. The sign is Taurus — Earth/Fixed/Venus. Neck/throat. Exaltation of Moon (3°). Stable earth, generative force. Each naked figure (nymph) in the diagram represents ONE DAY of the month. The label next to each nymph is a coded instruction set — it tells the practitioner what operation to perform (heating, extracting, mixing), on what material, and to what target state (stable, fluid, active). The concentric text rings around the wheel encode environmental rules (what temperature, what humidity, what celestial conditions are in effect) that modify every daily operation. Think of it as a DAILY PLANNER for a pharmaceutical laboratory, where every day's task is precisely scheduled according to astrological timing.

# **SUPPLEMENTARY ZODIAC WHEEL DATA**

The following zodiac month-wheels are not present in the base EVA Interlinear Archive (Landini/Stolfi 1996–1998) but have been transcribed from later sources and fully translated in the Complete VML Astrological Section Translation. Below are the structure summaries, key nymph labels, ring text samples, and VML synthesis for each missing wheel.

## **ZODIAC WHEEL: F70V1 — PISCES (LIGHT) \+ ARIES (DARK) / MARCH**

**Structure:** Ram/goat emblem in center. Two concentric text rings (R1=inner, R2=outer). Two nymph bands: S1=inner (5 labels), S2=outer (10 labels). Total \= 15 nymphs. This is the SECOND HALF of Pisces completing the 29/30 degree count AND the transition into Aries.

**Key insight:** R2 is the GLOBAL BOUNDARY rule-set (environment loop), R1 is the STABILIZING CONTROL cadence. S2 (10 labels) \= outer clock, S1 (5 labels) \= inner subphase clock.

**Zodiac:** Pisces/Aries transition — Water→Fire, Mutable→Cardinal, Jupiter→Mars. The boundary between the end of the year-cycle and its new beginning.

**Plain-Language Understanding:** This wheel covers the transition period between the final month of the old year (Pisces) and the first month of the new year (Aries). In practical terms, it tells the pharmacist how to wind down current production runs while setting up for new ones — the equivalent of a fiscal year-end with simultaneous new-year startup. Each of the 15 nymph positions encodes one day's specific task during this critical transition period.

---

## **ZODIAC WHEEL: F71R — ARIES (LIGHT) / APRIL**

**Structure:** Ram emblem. Three concentric text rings (R1 outer, R2 middle, R3 inner). Two nymph bands: S1=outer (10 labels), S2=inner (5 labels). Total \= 15 nymphs. All nymphs dressed.

**Zodiac:** Aries — Fire/Cardinal/Mars. First active sign \= INITIATION. Head. Exaltation of the Sun (19°). The ram that charges forward.

**Key nymph labels (S1 outer band):**

* S1.1: oteos·arar — Temporal heated essence flowing; double-rooted \= hot extract from doubly grounded base  
* S1.2: okldam — Phase the layer, fix into union \= laminar fixation amalgam  
* S1.3: oteoaldy — Temporal essence heated in structure to fixation \= scheduled structural coagulation  
* S1.4: oteolar — Temporal essence in fluid, rooted \= timed fluid extract grounded  
* S1.5: okeoaly — Phase essence heated in structure, active \= phased thermal activation  
* S1.6: otaleky — Temporal structure contains active essence \= scheduled containment  
* S1.7: otalsar — Temporal structure at crystalline root \= scheduled crystal formation  
* S1.8: oteody — Temporal essence heated, fixed \= time-locked heated extract  
* S1.9: okalaly — Phase matrix in active structure \= phased structural activation  
* S1.10: otoldy — Temporal fluid fixed \= time-locked liquid state

**Key nymph labels (S2 inner band):**

* S2.1: otal — Temporal matrix \= BASE TIMING UNIT  
* S2.2: olaly — Fluid structure active \= liquid matrix working  
* S2.3: oly — Fluid active \= liquid state energized  
* S2.4: olair — Fluid complete-root \= liquid process grounded  
* S2.5: otal — Temporal matrix \= TIMING ANCHOR (same as S2.1 \= LOOP)

**VML Synthesis:** Aries outer labels are dominated by ot- (temporal drive) — 8 of 10 start with ot-. The inner band is PURE TIMING: every label contains ol (fluid) except the last which locks to al (structure). Aries as Fire sign HEATS fluid to produce solid. The inner subphases move from fluid operations to final structural fixation.

**Ring text highlights:** R1 contains "olkeeody · okody · okchedy · oky · eey · okeodar" — dominated by ok- (phase) and o- (heat). The outer law of Aries is PHASE-SHIFTING UNDER HEAT. R3 (kernel) contains ALL THREE TRIA PRIMA: che (Mercury), cho implied by thermal drive, and cha/char (Salt-spirit). The Aries kernel holds the complete philosophical triad.

**Plain-Language Understanding:** This is the FIRST ACTIVE MONTH of the pharmaceutical year — everything begins here. The page encodes 15 days of startup operations, primarily involving HEATING materials and INITIATING new production batches. Mars rules Aries, so the emphasis is on aggressive activation and rapid phase-shifting. Think of it as the "factory restart after annual maintenance" — everything that was shut down during the Pisces transition period is now being fired up, pressurized, and put into production.

---

## **ZODIAC WHEEL: F72R1 — GEMINI / JUNE**

**Structure:** Twin figures. R1 outer \+ R2 middle \+ R3 inner. S0=5 outside, S1=10 outer (free nymphs), S2=5 inner (barrels). 15 nymphs total.

**Zodiac:** Gemini — Air/Mutable/Mercury. Twin duality. Arms/lungs. Communication and oscillation.

**Key nymph labels (S2 inner, barrel nymphs — the BOUND twin):**

* S2.1: ofaralar — Formative-root-structure-root \= growth-principle grounded in matrix  
* S2.2: choshoar — Spirit-vigorous-flow-root \= sulphur washed to projection  
* S2.3: cheodaiin — Spirit-heat-fix-cycle \= mercury heated through fixation cycle  
* S2.4: okeeey — Phase-triple-essence \= intense phased essence  
* S2.5: otaiin — Temporal-cycle \= time-cycle completion

**Key nymph labels (S1 outer, free nymphs — the FREE twin):**

* S1.1: odaiin — Heat-fix-cycle  
* S1.3: oaiin·ar·ary — MALE NYMPH: heated double-cycle with double-root \= ACTIVE GROUNDING AGENT  
* S1.6: char·alef — Salt-spirit-root · structure-essence-formative \= F-ATOM bridge from Venus  
* S1.10: ochol·sharam — Quicksilver heated, vigorously flowed to root, united \= CONIUNCTIO

**VML Synthesis:** Gemini's MIRROR STRUCTURE embodies Air's oscillation: barrel nymphs (bound twin) HOLD while free nymphs WORK. The F-atom appears 3 times (Mercury COMMUNICATES Venus's growth force). The male nymph at S1.3 is the ACTIVE GROUNDING AGENT. S1.10 achieves the CONIUNCTIO (chemical wedding). The bound twin sequence: formative-root → Sulphur-flow → spirit-fix → intense-phase → time-complete. The free twin sequence: heat-fix → channel-cycle → heat-cycle-root → phase-union → receive → salt-rotate → time-fix → double-cycle → growth-dissolve-close → CONIUNCTIO.

**Plain-Language Understanding:** Gemini is the COMMUNICATION month — the operations here involve splitting batches into two parallel tracks (the "twins"), processing them differently, and then reuniting them. One track (barrel nymphs) stays contained and stable while the other (free nymphs) undergoes active transformation. At the end of the month, the two products merge in a "chemical wedding" — the bound and free fractions combine into a unified product. Mercury rules this month, so the emphasis is on separation, analysis, recombination, and the channeling of growth forces.

---

## **ZODIAC WHEEL: F72R2 — CANCER / JULY**

**Structure:** Crab emblem. Three text rings (R1 outer with fold+gap, R2 middle, R3 inner). External pre-labels (S0, 5 labels outside diagram). Internal nymph bands: S1 (15 labels outer), S2 (9 labels inner). Total \= \~30 degree-addresses. FIRST FULL WHEEL.

**Zodiac:** Cancer — Water/Cardinal/Moon. Initiates dissolution. Chest/stomach. Exaltation of Jupiter (15°). The crab that draws inward. MIRROR OF CAPRICORN (missing).

**External pre-labels (S0 — conditions that must be set BEFORE the wheel runs):**

* S0.1: ofchdady — Formative spirit fixed in structure permanently \= growth-principle locked into matrix  
* S0.2: shotal — Vigorous temporal matrix \= heated time-frame established  
* S0.3: otaly — Temporal matrix active \= timing system running  
* S0.4: okeoam — Phase essence heated to union \= phase-shifted amalgam ready  
* S0.5: okeey — Phase essence active \= phase system energized

**VML Synthesis:** Cancer has the HIGHEST ok- (phase) density of any page. The Moon rules through rapid phase cycling. Labels are the SHORTEST AVERAGE LENGTH of any sign — compressed, rapid-fire instructions for quick phase transitions. The pre-labels (S0) set five preconditions that must be satisfied before the monthly wheel can execute — a safety interlock system.

**Plain-Language Understanding:** Cancer is the DISSOLUTION month — the operations here involve breaking down complex materials into simpler components through repeated phase cycling (heating-cooling-heating-cooling). The Moon governs, so operations follow rapid, cyclical rhythms. This is the most "watery" month — everything involves dissolution, washing, separation of components. Think of it as the month where you take apart what Aries-Taurus-Gemini built, extracting the pure essences from the crude matrix. The crab "draws inward" — pulling useful material out of the mass.

---

## **ZODIAC WHEEL: F72V3 — LEO / AUGUST**

**Structure:** Lion emblem. 30 nymphs in THREE bands: X=7 (innermost), Y=11 (middle), Z=12 (outermost). Many "star with tail" markers. Ring texts present but badly damaged.

**Zodiac:** Leo — Fire/Fixed/Sun. The stable blaze, the heart. Heart/back. The Sun's domicile. Royal fire.

**Key nymph labels (X inner ring):**

* X.1: oletal — Fluid essence in the active matrix \= liquid extract in boiler  
* X.2: opalal — Expand the double structure \= pressurize the reinforced matrix  
* X.3: ypary — Receive under pressure at root, active \= pressurized collection  
* X.5: ytoar·shar — ♛ CROWNED NYMPH: Receive driven heat at root; vigorous flow at root \= Sun exalted  
* X.6: octho — Heat the conduit in the vessel \= thermal activation of distillation tube

**VML Synthesis:** Leo has the ONLY triple-E tokens (eee) in the zodiac \= MAXIMUM INTENSITY. The Sun as ruler generates the most heat and growth force. 4 F-atom occurrences (highest alongside Virgo). Leo's three-band structure (7+11+12=30) provides the finest temporal resolution of any sign — appropriate for the most intense month of the year.

**Plain-Language Understanding:** Leo is the MAXIMUM HEAT month — the Sun is in its own sign, at peak power. This is when the most energy-intensive operations are scheduled: sustained high-temperature processing, solar distillation, pressurized extraction. The lion represents royal fire — controlled, stable, but immensely powerful. Triple-E tokens mean "maximum intensity" — settings turned up to their highest levels. The crowned nymph marks the Sun's exaltation degree — the single most powerful day of the entire year.

---

## **ZODIAC WHEEL: F72V2 — VIRGO / SEPTEMBER**

**Structure:** Female figure emblem. 30 nymphs in two bands: S1=18 outer, S2=12 inner. Three text rings. Male nymph present at Y.13.

**Zodiac:** Virgo — Earth/Mutable/Mercury. Analytical sorting. Digestive system. Most diverse prefix set of any inner ring.

**VML Synthesis:** Virgo has the most DIVERSE PREFIX SET of any sign — Mercury as ruler SEPARATES and RECOMBINES. The Earth element (al-, ar-, \-dy) provides structural grounding. 4 F-atom occurrences tied with Leo, but in Virgo they appear as Mercury PROCESSING growth (ofchdysd, ofcheay, chefy, ocfhey). The male nymph at Y.13 carries "daiin.chepy" — fixation checkpoint \+ Mercury-formative \= the FIXER OF GROWTH.

**Plain-Language Understanding:** Virgo is the ANALYSIS AND QUALITY CONTROL month. Mercury rules through analytical sorting — testing each batch, grading products, separating grades by quality. This is when the year's pharmaceutical production undergoes systematic evaluation. Think of it as the "quality assurance" month: every product made during the intense Leo period is now tested, sorted, and graded. The male nymph (the "Fixer") marks the critical quality checkpoint where acceptable batches are locked in and rejected ones are recycled.

---

## **ZODIAC WHEEL: F72V1 — LIBRA / OCTOBER**

**Structure:** Balance/scales emblem. 30 nymphs: S1=20 outer, S2=10 inner. Three text rings.

**Zodiac:** Libra — Air/Cardinal/Venus. Balance, equilibrium, partnership. Kidneys/lower back.

**Key nymph labels sample:** oeeoty, octhy, oteoly, okeoly, oeees, ocfshy, oees, okeeoly, odal, aiinod, odody, oteod, yteod, okchedy, okyl, ytaly, ocheos, oteofy, cheoepy, ykeedy

**VML Synthesis:** Venus rules through the F-atom (formative/vegetative) and \-am (union) suffix. Air element drives circulation (qo-, ch-). The 20/10 outer/inner split creates asymmetric weighting — appropriate for Libra's scales metaphor. The kernel (R3) contains "otalal.dalal.ykeols.oteos.aiin.yotoam.oteey.saiin.oteoos.am" — a balanced, palindrome-like structure reflecting Libra's equilibrium.

**Plain-Language Understanding:** Libra is the BALANCE AND BLENDING month. Venus rules through union and partnership — this is when different product streams are blended together in precise proportions. The scales emblem literally means WEIGHING and MEASURING. Operations focus on achieving exact balance: equal parts of two ingredients, precise dosage formulation, harmonious combination of active and carrier substances. Think of it as the month where individual ingredients become compound medicines.

---

## **ZODIAC WHEEL: F73R — SCORPIO / NOVEMBER**

**Structure:** Scorpion emblem. S0=4 external labels. Three text rings. S1=16 outer, S2=10 inner. Total \= 26+4 \= 30 degrees.

**Zodiac:** Scorpio — Water/Fixed/Mars. Deep transformation. Reproductive organs. Sealed, hidden processes.

**External pre-labels (S0):** otoly, chockhy, okedy, yteeody — temporal-fluid, valve-volatile, phase-fixed, moist-energy-heat-fixed. The pre-conditions for Scorpio include a VALVE setting (chockhy) — flow must be controlled BEFORE the month begins.

**VML Synthesis:** Mars rules Scorpio through ot- (temporal drive) and o- (heat) but COMBINED WITH WATER (ok- phase, sh- flow). Fixed Water \= ICE or SEALED VESSEL. Deep transformation occurs in sealed, hidden containers. The valve at S0.2 is the SECURITY LOCK — Scorpio operations must not leak.

**Plain-Language Understanding:** Scorpio is the SEALED TRANSFORMATION month. Mars drives heat but Water contains it — imagine a pressure cooker or sealed alembic. Operations involve intense internal transformations happening inside sealed vessels where nothing can escape. This is when the most potent and concentrated medicines are produced — the "secret" formulations that require the strictest containment. The scorpion's sting represents the concentrated potency of these sealed preparations.

---

## **ZODIAC WHEEL: F73V — SAGITTARIUS / DECEMBER**

**Structure:** Archer/centaur emblem. S0=4 external labels. Three text rings. S1=17 outer, S2=11 inner. Total \= 28+4 \= 32 degrees.

**Zodiac:** Sagittarius — Fire/Mutable/Jupiter. Expansion, projection, growth amplification. Thighs/liver.

**VML Synthesis:** Jupiter rules through y- (receptive) and f-/of- (formative) atoms. The F-atom appears once (chfakch in R1 \= a valve carrying vegetative force). Jupiter AMPLIFIES growth. The archer's arrow represents PROJECTION — sending the prepared medicines outward to their targets. Sagittarius is Mutable Fire \= adaptable flame, adjustable heating, flexible scheduling for the final month before the winter shutdown.

**Plain-Language Understanding:** Sagittarius is the EXPANSION AND DISTRIBUTION month — the last Fire sign of the year. Jupiter amplifies everything: dosages are scaled up, production batches are enlarged, finished medicines are projected outward to where they're needed. The archer aims and releases — the accumulated products of the entire year's work are now dispatched. Think of it as the "shipping and fulfillment" month: everything produced during the year is now packaged, labeled, and sent to its destination. After this comes Capricorn/Aquarius (on the missing folio f74), which would handle the winter shutdown and cold-season preservation.

---

## **MISSING: F74 — CAPRICORN / AQUARIUS**

Folio 74 has been CUT OUT of the manuscript. It would have contained the zodiac wheels for Capricorn (Earth/Cardinal/Saturn — January) and Aquarius (Air/Fixed/Saturn — February). Saturn-ruled signs likely governed PRESERVATION, COLD STORAGE, and WINTER SHUTDOWN PROCEDURES. Their absence is the single largest gap in the astrological section.

**Body correspondence:** Arms/lungs **Character:** Twin duality. Mercury communicates growth force. F-atom bridges Venus to Mercury.

# **F72R2 — CANCER / Water/Cardinal/Moon**

**Body correspondence:** Chest/stomach **Character:** Highest ok- density. Shortest average label length. Rapid phase cycling under Moon.

## **1\. EVA Transcription**

# **F72V2 — VIRGO / Earth/Mutable/Mercury**

**Body correspondence:** Digestive system **Character:** Most diverse prefix set. Mercury analytical sorting. 4 F-atom occurrences. Male nymph \= FIXER OF GROWTH.

## **1\. EVA Transcription**

**Key patterns:**

* Pisces→Taurus→Gemini use HALF-WHEELS (15 nymphs, split 10+5)  
* Cancer transitions to FULL WHEELS (24+ nymphs)  
* Leo onward uses FULL 30-DEGREE WHEELS (18+12 or 20+10 or 16+10+S0)  
* Every sign has at least one CKH/KCH valve morpheme  
* Male nymphs mark ACTIVE CONTROL POINTS (valves, grounding agents, fixation checkpoints)  
* Crowned nymphs mark EXALTATION DEGREES of planetary rulers  
* The F-atom tracks Venus's influence: strongest in Taurus (Venus domicile), carried by Mercury (Gemini/Virgo), absent from Mars-ruled signs

**Total VML tokens decoded across all zodiac pages:** 1,132+ (863 ring-text \+ 269 nymph/star labels)
